 My dearest Navya and Aaradhya
 
 
 tum donon apane najuk kandhon par behad beshkeemtee viraasaton ko lekar chal rahi ho - aradhya - tumhaare paas he tumhaare pardada dow harivanshrai bachchan kii viraasat, or navya - tumhaare paas tumhaare pardada echpi nanda kii viraasat he
 
 
 Your great-grandfathers recognized, respected and brought fame to your existing family names (surname)
 
 
 ! You both can be Nanda or Bachchan, but you are also girls, women
 
 
 ! 
 
 
 or chunki tum mahila ho, log apni soch, apni simaaen tum par thopenge
 
 
 They will tell you, what dress you should wear, how you should behave, who you should meet, where you should go, or where not
 
 
 logon ke faislon kii chaaya main na rahanaa
 
 
 Make your own decisions with your understanding
 
 
 kisi ko bhi tumhen yah ehsaas mat dilaane dena ki tumhaari skirt kii lambaai se tumhaare charitra ko jaancha yaa mapa ja saktaa he
 
 
 With whom you should befriend, do not decide your friends with the advice of anyone else
 
 
 shaadi sirf isi vajah se karnaa, kyonki tum aisa karnaa chaahati ho, kisi bhi or vajah se nahin
 
 
 People will talk
 
 
 ve bahut buree baaten bhi kahenge
 
 
 But this does not mean that you have to listen to everyone
 
 
 kabhi is baat kii chintaa mat karnaa - log kya kahenge
 
 
 ! aakhirkaar, tumhen hi apane faislon kaa acha-bura parinaam bhugatna hoga, so, kisi bhi or ko apane faisle mat karne dena
 
 
 Navya - The special recognition that you get from your name and family name, can not save you from the problems that you will have to face as a woman
 
 
 lekin nakaaratmakataa ko khud ko niraash-hataash mat karne dena, kyonki insaan main bahut-si achchhaaiyaan bhi baaki hai
 
 
 Aaradhya - As long as you are able to read and understand this letter, i might not stay here, but my understanding says that whatever i am saying, it will still be relevant
 
 
 mahilaon ke liye is duniya main jeena bahut-bahut mushkil ho saktaa he, lekin mujhe vishwaas he ki tum jaisi mahilaayein hi in halaat ko badal daalengi
 
 
 It will not be easy for you to set your own boundaries, make your own decisions, rise above denying people's decisions
 
 
 lekin tum
 
 
 You can set an example for women all over the world
 
 
 aisa kar dikhaao, or tumhaari uplabdhi meri sari umr kii uplabdhiyon se kahin zyaada sabit hogi
 
 
 And it would be a great honor for me not to be known as Amitabh Bachchan, but as your grandfather and grandfather
 
 
 tippaniyan All my love 
 
 tumhaara dadaji, tumhaara naanaa Both of you are carrying on your delicate shoulders the most precious legacies - Aaradhya - you have the legacy of your great-grandfather Dr
 Harivanshrai Bachchan, and Navya - you have the legacy of your great-grandfather HP Nanda
 
 
 tum donon ke pardaadaon ne tumhaare maujuuda paariwarik naamon (surname) ko pahchaan, sammaan or shoharat di
 
 
 ! tum donon nanda yaa bachchan ho sakati ho, lekin tum ladkiyaan bhi ho, mahila
 
 
 ! 
 
 
 And since you are a woman, people will impose their thinking, their limitations on you
 
 
 ve tumhen bataaenge, tumhen kisi poshaak pahanani chahie, tumhen kaise bartaav karnaa chahie, tumhen kisase milanaa chahie, tumhen kahaan janaa chahie, kahaan nahin
 
 
 Do not remain in the shadow of people's decisions
 
 
 apni samaj se apane faisle khud karnaa
 
 
 Don't let anyone make you realize that your skirt can be tested or measured by the length of your skirt
 
 
 tumhen kisase dosti kerani chahie, ise lekar kisi bhi or kii salaah se apane dost tay nahin karnaa
 
 
 Get married only because you want to do it, not for any other reason
 
 
 log baaten karenge
 
 
 They will also say very bad things
 
 
 lekin iskaa arth yah nahin he ki tumhen sabaki sunani hogi
 
 
 Never worry about what people will say
 
 
 ! After all, you will have to suffer good or bad consequences of your decisions, so do not let anyone else make your decisions
 
 
 navya - tumhaare naam or paariwarik naam se jo vishesh pahchaan tumhen hasil he, vah tumhen un pareshaaniyon se nahin bachaa saktin, jinka saamana tumhen mahila hone ke naate karnaa hoga
 
 
 But don't let negativity disappoint you, because there are many good things left in man
 
 
 aradhya - jab tak tum is khat ko padhane or samajhane laayak hovogi, tab tak main shaayad yahaan na rahun, lekin meri samaj kahati he ki jo kuch bhi main kah rahaa hum, vah tab bhi praasangik hoga

 is dauraan paatra ne bataaya ki rajasthan kin-kin kshetron main awwal he or kin kshetron main rajasthan pratham rahaa he
 According to Patra, these are the areas where Rajasthan is far ahead of other states of India
 
 
 - rajasthan sarkaar kii yojana bhamashah yojana main 1 karod 57 lakh parivaar or kareeb 5 karod logon ko free ilaaj card dene main rajasthan pehle sthaan par he

 - 400 se adhik sarkari yojanaayen kii electronic dilvari dene ke liye rajasthan pratham he
 Rajasthan ranks first in opening 6700 Annapurna Bhandar
 - pratham jaitun rifinary kholane kaa kaary rajasthan main hua
 - For the first time RSUI was established in Rajasthan
 - sahakaari sansthaanon main chunaav ke liye shaikshanik yogyata lagu karne vaale pehla rajya bana rajasthan
 Rajasthan is the first state to start a petrol refinery in the public sector
 - naveen pension yojana main sarvaadhik 9 hajaar karod rupee se adhik raashi dene main rajasthan pehle number par rahaa

 da tribune akhbaar ne grih mantralay ke sutron ke hawaale se bataaya ki in 23 rohingyaon kii pahchaan kar lee gai he

 assam police ne inrohingyaonki suchi bhi saajha kii he
